Erniu looked at the grapes, and suddenly felt an immeasurable sense of longing. Thumping his chest, he said, “Senior, I can tell the fire’s about to go out. I’m good at stoking fires. I have strong lungs!”

Erniu hurried over, squatted next to the fire, and started blowing on the flames. The old man looked at the two of them and smiled mysteriously. He did nothing to stop either of them. And thus, Xu Qing and Erniu worked hard together to roast the grapes.

The first skewer went to the old man. As for the second skewer, Xu Qing turned to look at his Eldest Brother, who had been working very hard.

“Go ahead and give it to him,” the old man said casually.

Erniu excitedly took a skewer of roasted grapes from Xu Qing and started eating. His eyes shone.

When Xu Qing reached the last skewer, he took a deep breath and started eating the grapes. Rumbling filled him, and as his soul reached a state of being completely full, it rose to a higher level. His godsource also started seething. As of now, there was no sound other than that of the eating and the swallowing of food. Sometime later, Xu Qing was truly unable to eat anything further. However, seeing that his Eldest Brother wasn’t done, he handed him the half skewer he had left over.

Erniu excitedly took it and started wolfing down the grapes.

As the old man watched, he rubbed his belly and got to his feet. “Given how we met here, I’d say we’re connected by destiny. I’m here waiting for a little something to arrive. Once it’s here, I’ll be leaving.” He looked at Xu Qing and Erniu. “You’re not members of my clan, but you are human. The world you live in managed to attract the attention of Eminent Desolation.... It’s hard to say if that’s a good thing or a bad thing for the living things in your world. As for you, boy....”

He focused on Xu Qing. “It was a member of the elder generation who crafted that fleshly body for you, am I right? Whoever it was, they were very daring. The method used was wild and bold. That said, you shouldn’t have come to the Primeval Sea. Now that you’re here, your aura could easily spread to all the star rings. That’s why I noticed you when you arrived.

“I wanted to see for myself this body of yours that was created with the flesh of Eminent Desolation. It really is an unprecedented path. Unfortunately, the humans in your world don’t know very much about the Primeval Sea. Therefore, you don’t know why you shouldn’t come here. So it’s all very understandable.”

As the old man spoke, his eyes gleamed with admiration. “You have good character, boy. You know how to be helpful, not just take advantage of others. You also worked hard, Fur Monster. Ah, whatever. I guess I might as well help you get rid of some of that filth on you.”

The old man waved his hand. Instantly, a wind of flames rushed toward Xu Qing and Erniu.

An instant later, Xu Qing heard a scream of anguish from behind him. Two shadowy figures materialized out of both him and Erniu. The hot wind sent them spinning backward, until they were floating some distance away. The two soul shadows merged, turning into the little girl that they had run into at the very beginning of their sea journey. It hadn’t actually left them! Upon appearing, the girl looked in terror at the old man.

“Screw off,” the old man said coolly.

The girl shivered and disappeared.

Xu Qing and the Captain were shaken. Rising to their feet, they clasped hands thankfully. Of course, they had countless questions that they wanted to ask.

However, that was when the old man suddenly looked up into the sky. A faint smile appeared on his face. “The little thing I’ve been waiting for is about to arrive.”

Almost in unison with the words spoken by the old man, the dusky interior of the world inside Timeruins suddenly flared with shimmering, dazzling light. It was magnificent, almost like light refracted off the surface of water, which then rippled up to illuminate the canopy of heaven with multi-colored brightness. Meanwhile, the swampy lands were also changing in a mysterious way. Dense water vapor billowed out of nowhere, rapidly covering the entire swamp, and significantly reducing visibility.

Xu Qing and Erniu looked around with shocked expressions on their faces. Before either could do a thing, a heaven-rending, earth-crushing sound erupted, like the howl of a beast or the roar of a god.

Next, a massive river appeared, with waves that carried time itself as it rushed in their direction. In the blink of an eye, it rushed right past Xu Qing and Erniu, and then disappeared into something like a black hole some 30,000 meters away.

It was as if the river Xu Qing and Erniu could see was only one small section of a much mightier river. The water came from heaven, flowed past them, then disappeared 30,000 meters away, where it went to a different section of time.

Even more gruish was that, even though the water of the river rushed rapidly right in front of them, it didn’t actually seem to be located in the same dimension as them. The flowing water seemed illusory, as if this was just a reflection that had appeared for some reason in their location.

Xu Qing immediately recognized what he was looking at. “The River of Time!”

Wherever time passed, this river existed. However, to make it appear required either very unique authority or astonishing levels of power. Xu Qing had experience with this river, whether it was Princess Brightblossom in the Moonrite Region or other gods who had time abilities. All of them took the initiative to use it, causing the great river to appear, and then borrowing its power to fish out time from within it. All of them were using it.

But what was happening with this old man, who apparently came from some world beyond theirs, was completely different. The old man stood in the middle of the River of Time, looking at the spot where it came from. He was clearly waiting. He was waiting for the ‘little thing’ that he had mentioned.... It seemed that, in his eyes, the great River of Time wasn’t something mysterious or profound. It was as if he could calculate its flow with ease, and understand all of its karma. Apparently... he was standing within time itself, waiting for some sort of prey to appear. This was a level that completely surpassed the concept of simply using the river.

Thanks to Xu Qing’s god perception, his mind and heart were pulsing in sync with the river. It made him think about back when he gained enlightenment of the authority of sound. Godly authority was something primeval that came from primal-chaos itself. It was an extremely ancient power that existed within the dark recesses of the world. Merely being able to grasp it signified that one was qualified to use it. And that would create a sealing mark.

But that only related to using it. This was a much higher level that revolved around control. As Xu Qing looked at this old man and considered these matters, he came to the conclusion... that the old man was definitely at that level! Maybe he wasn’t a god, but he was able to do things that ordinary gods couldn’t do.

That was the limit of what Xu Qing could ‘see.’ However, he was also certain that this was not the limit of what this old man could do. As for where his limits were, the details would differ based on perception. Perhaps to most living beings, it would be enough to say that the old man was ‘strong.’

Meanwhile, Erniu was also reeling in mind and heart.

As the two of them dealt with a myriad of conflicting emotions and thoughts, a stream of golden light appeared in the great River of Time. The light sped through the water, moving much faster than the flow of the river itself. And wherever it passed, the waves of time collapsed.

Upon seeing that, Xu Qing yet again felt his mind teetering.

There’s something inside the River of Time moving faster than the river itself...? Doesn’t that imply that this golden light can move faster than time?

Everything Xu Qing had seen and experienced in the outer sea had shattered his previous conceptions of the world. His eyes had truly been opened to new horizons.

As he watched something move faster than time itself, Xu Qing’s heart started racing. He wanted to see clearly what that golden light was, but clearly, his current level of cultivation base wouldn’t allow him to do so.

But then... the golden light speeding through the river reached the old man. There, it stopped, moving no further. And its true form was revealed. When Xu Qing saw it clearly, his eyes went wide. Erniu's gaze became one of great curiosity.

It was a golden rat! It looked very similar to the golden rat Xu Qing and Erniu had encountered in that cave when they acquired the holy fardark nectar. That said, its aura was different. Furthermore, this golden rat pulsed with an even more ancient aura. One thing was for certain, it was definitely a member of the same species![1]

As for this golden rat, it didn’t run around on four legs. Instead, it walked upright like a human. A single hemp sandal hung from its mouth, which it held in both hands. Apparently, it had been running along and chewing the sandal at the same time, resulting in the sandal being somewhat dilapidated.

The moment the rat saw the old man, a look of surprise and fear appeared on its face. Its eyes shone with terror, and it immediately stopped chewing on the sandal. The golden rat then spun around and fled in the opposite direction, going against the flow of the river. freewebnovel.com

The old man looked at the golden rat and smiled. “Little thing, you stole something of mine. I let you run free for quite a while, but now here you are right in front of me!”

The old man reached out through the River of Time to grab the rat.

A series of anxious squeals erupted from the mouth of the golden rat. At the same time, golden light shone off it, turning the surrounding river a golden color as it accelerated dramatically. It really seemed like it would manage to speed against the flow of the river and disappear into the canopy of heaven.

But only an instant later, the old man’s grasping hand caused the spot where the river came out of the sky to be sealed off. The same thing happened to the area where it disappeared into the earth 30,000 meters away. Both ends had been sealed. The river now couldn’t flow in this area!

The golden rat’s path was sealed both ahead and behind! The river water in between those spots was cut off and began to sink down.

The golden rat shivered as it tried to break into the void. But an instant later, the river water that remained behind surged, becoming a rope of water that shot toward the rat. The rope ignored the struggles of the rat, wrapping tightly around its neck and dragging it toward the old man.

In the blink of an eye, it landed in the old man’s hand. He shook it back and forth.

Perhaps the rope of river water was too tight, or perhaps it was just terrifyingly powerful. Either way, the rat’s legs trembled and it squeaked several times. Pale froth bubbled at its lips, and its eyes went blank before fluttering shut. Its life force was rapidly vanishing, and an aura of death spread through it. Soon, it wasn’t moving at all, making it seem like it was dead.

Erniu, meanwhile, blinked a few times and then suddenly shouted, “Senior, that rogue is just pretending to be dead! Hmmmphh! I can’t believe someone would try to fake their own death in front of me! I can tell the truth at a glance. This little thing is just too inexperienced!”

A faint smile appeared on the old man’s face as he looked at the golden rat hanging limply in his hand. “Even Fur Monster can see that you’re pretending to be dead. Very clumsy indeed. If you want to get out of this alive, you’re going to have to help me.”

The golden rat shivered from head to toe and then opened its eyes. After casting a murderous glare at Erniu, it shifted its gaze to the old man, making sure to look very flattering.

Then it lifted up the hemp sandal with both hands, as if formally returning it.

The old man took the sandal, noting its dilapidated state. After shaking it out a few times, he dropped it onto the ground and slipped his foot into it. He shook his head.

“You good-for-nothing lout. Last time you stole my clothing, I took away your ability to speak. Then you coveted my sandals, and after going to all the effort of stealing one, you only managed to eat this much of it? I guess you’re just not very lucky.”

With that, the old man gripped the rope of time that was tied around the rat’s neck, and started walking up toward the dome of heaven. The rat swayed back and forth, looking very pitiful. At a certain point, it looked down at Erniu with a scowl, as if it was determined to remember what he looked like.

Xu Qing wasn’t paying attention to the rat. He kept his eyes on the old man, all while wondering if he should ask the questions that burned inside of him right now.

When Erniu noticed the golden rat glaring at him, he laughed coldly in his heart. He had to agree with what the old grandpa said, that this rat was really unlucky. After chewing on that hemp sandal, it hardly managed to swallow more than a bite or two. Erniu knew that if he had that opportunity, he would have stuffed the entire thing into his stomach. He looked back at the rat with clear derision.

The golden rat got even angrier at that, and let loose some more squeaks.

The old man heard and laughed. “You sense the bloodline of one of your descendants? Well, of course! Otherwise, these two wouldn’t have been swallowed by Timeruins and arrived in the very spot where I was waiting for you. Okay, enough tattle-telling. We need to go home.”

The old man was almost at the horizon now, where he waved his right hand gently toward the dome of heaven. The sky rumbled loudly. Great cracking sounds rang out as the sky split open, revealing a massive rift.... The other side of the rift was pitch black, but it was clearly possible to detect the aura of another world. It was above the surface of a sea!

The old man took another step forward. He was about to go through the rift.

Xu Qing suddenly clasped hands and bowed, all while speaking in a loud voice. “Senior, there’s something I’m confused about. If you’re inclined to explain, I would greatly appreciate it. Earlier, you said that this place is the Primeval Sea. And you said that the world my Elder Brother and I are from doesn’t know much about the Primeval Sea. In that case... what is the Primeval Sea? And why would my aura be sensed by all of the star rings?”

Xu Qing remained bowed at the waist as he waited for an answer.

The old man turned around and looked at Xu Qing. “You have a body made from Eminent Desolation’s flesh, so you should at least have a vague sense of the fact that the universe we all occupy has thirty-six star rings. Every star ring is vast and boundless, and filled with countless lands and places.[2]

“The Primeval Sea is a fantastic thing. Any location where it exists is a strategic spot and a prosperous place. And that’s because the Primeval Sea connects all of the star rings in the universe. And that’s also why, when you come here, your aura can spread everywhere.

“That said, don’t worry. I made sure to cover your aura. What’s more, the Primeval Sea in this spot is special. It’s currently sealed. You can only get in through rifts, which means that outsiders can never stay inside for very long. After all, your star ring used to be extremely famous.

“I suppose our meeting indicates we have a predestined affinity. One day, if you ever become a Lower Immortal, then you’ll have the basic qualifications to pass through the Primeval Sea. If you use that opportunity to leave this place, and if you’re also willing, you can use the Primeval Sea to come find me in the Immortal Capital in the Fifth Star Ring. That’s a world ruled by humans, and it’s also a world of immortals.”

With that, the old man stepped through the rift and vanished.

1. The golden rat first appeared in chapter 922, and was in every chapter until the most relevant aspect of that small story arc, which was in chapter 927. ☜

2. We have previously heard about ‘star rings’ in chapters 642, 705 (the footnote here might be worth revisiting if you don’t remember what I said about it), and 899. This term is not a very common term. Of the roughly 20+ dictionaries I use, only one of them has a definition of it (only in Chinese, and it’s not a very detailed definition, being only an explanation from a random line of ancient poetry). There isn’t even a Baidu wiki entry for the term, and Baidu wiki has entries for just about everything. If you do an image search of it, you will find some images of the planet Saturn. This is because the character “star” can also mean planet depending on the context. You can also find pictures of galaxies. This is not the common word for galaxy. However, in my imagination, these ‘star rings’ look like galaxies, and based on how they are described here and later, that seems to me to be the most plausible interpretation of what they look like. This is a fantasy universe, so I don’t in any way think that they are supposed to correspond to what real-life galaxies are, in terms of the number of stars/planets in them, or anything like that. ☜

In the world inside Timeruins, Xu Qing and Erniu looked up at the rift in the dome of heaven, a thousand thoughts running through their minds.

To Xu Qing, this experience in the outer sea had been both freakish and phenomenal. That included the gruish entities they had encountered, and this human old man. All of them were deeply thought-provoking. The words the old man spoke before leaving had truly opened Xu Qing’s eyes to the world, and left him feeling deeply shaken.

Thirty-six star rings... and the Primeval Sea.... There were some things that Xu Qing had come to vaguely sense upon acquiring this body created from Eminent Desolation’s flesh. For instance, he did have a vague impression that there were thirty-six star rings out there. However, this was his first time hearing about the Primeval Sea. I can’t rule out that what he told me is false. But in all likelihood, it seems true....

Off to the side, Erniu slapped his thigh. “Little Ah Qing,” he said in a serious tone, “I’ve finally figured it out!”

Xu Qing looked over. He was curious to hear his Eldest Brother’s thoughts. After all, this elderly human who proclaimed himself to be from the Immortal Capital in the Fifth Star Ring was too shocking, both in terms of his cultivation base and his manner of speaking. ‘Outrageous’ was a perfectly acceptable word to use to describe him.

With a grave facial expression, Erniu looked at Xu Qing and said, “Up on the surface of the sea, all I had to do was say the word ‘safe,’ and we would instantly encounter some really freakish things.... Now that I think about it, it was obviously the doings of that old man! He did it all on purpose!”

Erniu looked a bit disappointed, as if he really had believed that everything which happened was a direct result of the words that left his mouth. Apparently, his thoughts had been focused elsewhere. Unlike Xu Qing, he hadn’t been paying close attention to the old man’s final words, and their astonishing implications. Xu Qing was of course used to the way that his Eldest Brother’s way of thinking differed from that of normal people.

That venerable Senior said that humans rule the Fifth Star Ring. It’s a world of immortals.... Of course, I can’t just automatically trust everything he says.

Xu Qing looked at the distant rift in the dome of heaven. It was hard to say if Erniu had really missed that last bit of information, or if he just wasn’t shocked by it.

As Xu Qing stared up into the sky, Erniu looked over at the spot where the old man had dropped his sandal onto the ground. Leaping over to that spot, he squatted down and started searching the area. Before long, he managed to locate four strips of woven hemp.

Erniu’s eyes gleamed with mad joy as he picked them up, handling them as if they were precious treasures. He immediately put them into his mouth and bit down with his teeth. A moment later, he frowned, as he realized that biting the hemp wasn’t doing anything. As he kept trying in different ways, he noticed that Xu Qing seemed to be lost in thought. He blinked a few times.

“Don’t waste your brainpower, little Ah Qing. Those things aren’t even relevant to us. Besides, we have no way of knowing if that old fellow had good intentions or malicious ones. If you ask me, he didn’t just want to have a look at you. He was probably interested in forming some karmic bonds with us! Otherwise, why would he offer us that skewered meat?”

Xu Qing nodded. “Eldest Brother, just now you said we had no way of knowing if that human Senior had good intentions or malicious ones. You clearly don’t suspect the accuracy of the things he said....” Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. “I guess that means... you already knew about all that stuff he told us?”

Erniu cleared his throat. Little Ah Qing just keeps getting more and more wily. It’s really hard to fool him nowadays.

Erniu laughed heartily, glanced left and right, and then looked at Xu Qing with shining eyes. “There’s no need to get into all of that. Say, did it occur to you that we also have a golden rat like that one we just saw? Remember, Little Jianjian is incubating those eggs. In fact, I wonder if they’ve hatched already. Wait, hold on. This won’t do. Considering how incredible that golden rat was, I’d say we have to get back to the imperial capital post haste. We need to get those little rats back from Wu Jianwu!”[1]

Xu Qing didn’t reply, but he kept his eyes on Erniu.

Seeing that, Erniu again tried to change the topic. Waving the four hemp threads in Xu Qing’s direction, he said, “Look at these hemp threads! Considering that golden rat was so interested in them, they must be treasures! I just tried to take a bite, but these thingies are just too tough! I couldn’t even leave a dent!” Erniu looked down at the hemp threads. “Of course, that old rat was a complete idiot. Just because you can’t bite them doesn’t mean you can’t eat them!”

Erniu suddenly looked very proud. “It’s not like I’ve never encountered unbitable things before. In situations like this, I know exactly what to do!”

He gritted his teeth. Considering that he really wanted to distract Xu Qing, he decided to throw caution to the wind.

As Xu Qing watched, Erniu placed his hand on his belly, then shoved violently. Unexpectedly, blood sprayed everywhere as he ripped his abdomen open. Then, he placed two of the hemp threads directly into his stomach. Having done that, he pulled the flaps of ripped belly flesh closed like a garment. Then he used the black fur growing off his skin to tie the pieces together. He tossed the other two hemp threads to Xu Qing.

“I might not know what they taste like, but as you can see, I still managed to get them into my stomach.” Looking very pleased with himself, the Captain patted his belly.

Xu Qing sighed. His Eldest Brother hadn’t directly answered the questions, but his actions gave Xu Qing the information he sought. And he was confident that there was a good reason for his Eldest Brother not wanting to say such things out loud....

With such thoughts in mind, Xu Qing decided not to ask any more questions. Taking the two hemp threads, he studied them before putting them into his bag of holding. Then, looking very calm, he said, “Let’s go.”

Erniu sighed inwardly in relief when he saw that Xu Qing wasn’t asking any further questions. Nodding vigorously, he flew with Xu Qing up into the air and toward the rift. When they passed through the rift, they left the world inside Timeruins, and found themselves on the surface of the outer sea.

Even upon leaving Timeruins, Xu Qing didn’t get a good look at the thing’s true features. It was as if the moment they flew out, Timeruins melted back into the sea like an ink painting, ultimately vanishing in very gruish fashion.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered profoundly. He finally took out his dreadnaught, boarded, and looked off into the depths of the outer sea, all the while thinking about the Fifth Star Ring that old man had mentioned.

The surface of the sea was as calm and silent as death.

Erniu stood next to him, and when he noticed what Xu Qing was looking at, he sighed inwardly again.

“Seriously, little Junior Brother. Stop thinking about it. When you asked me if I knew about that stuff, I didn’t answer your question. Not because I didn’t want to tell you, but because I just can’t say the name of the place you’re thinking about. That name is taboo. Inauspicious.

“I’ve never seen that old man before, neither in this life nor in any of my past lives. But as soon as he mentioned the name of that place, I got an idea of who he might be.

“This isn’t his first time appearing in Revered Ancient. Master probably knows something about the old man. In fact, Master is the one who told me about the taboo and inauspicious nature of that name. Countless years in the past, Master ran a very thorough investigation and told me that the old man actually showed up in Revered Ancient two times in the past.

“The first time was when he appeared to the Summer Immortals and told them about the Fifth Star Ring. Later, the Summer Immortals left, presumably to go to that place, except they’ve never returned.

“The second time, according to Master’s suspicions, was before Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity left. Incidentally, both Master and Empress Summer Departure believe that Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity is no longer with the holy lands. So where is he?

“Today was the third time, and he came either for you or me.

“As for the place he came from, that name... at least according to Master... doesn’t actually exist. However, when people hear it spoken of, it gains foundation in reality. In other words, the more people talk about it, the more real it becomes.”

Xu Qing turned to look at Erniu. Erniu looked at Xu Qing.

After a moment of thought, Xu Qing said, “And what do you think, Eldest Brother?”

Erniu looked off into the distance for a long moment. He shook his head. “Master’s theory makes sense, and I agree with part of it. But there’s part of it I’m not sure about. After all, Master has never been there.

“I have the feeling that the place is real. The question is whether it’s good or evil. In this universe of gods, there are many, many fantastic things. Anything can exist. Everything is possible. A good example is me.”

That last sentence struck Xu Qing like a bolt of heavenly thunder, filling his mind with rumbling sounds and causing him to breathe heavily. In fact, compared to that bit of information, everything else didn’t seem very important to Xu Qing. Xu Qing still didn’t know who his Eldest Brother really was. However, given everything they had been through, and all the gruish things he had seen his Eldest Brother do, Xu Qing had some speculations.

“Eldest Brother, you....” Xu Qing trailed off.

Erniu didn’t say anything for a long moment, and his eyes shone with uncharacteristic confusion. “Little Junior Brother, there are some people who call me a god bastard. Some people call me a monstrous freak.... As for what I really am, Master doesn’t know, and neither do I. The truth is that I’ve been searching for an answer all along.[2]

“I can remember time passing by and being resurrected over and over again. And there are some things about my past that, when I recall them, I forget things from the present. In truth... there are already some things about this life, even habits, that I’ve forgotten. I truly fear that the day could come, little Junior Brother... that I don’t recognize you. Or Master.... It wouldn’t be until the following life that, in a sudden flash, I remember all of you.”

Erniu’s voice grew softer and softer as he spoke.

Meanwhile, an indescribable feeling built up in Xu Qing. He wasn’t sure exactly what it was, but it felt bitter and painful.

Erniu noticed Xu Qing’s facial expression, and for a brief moment, a look of pride flashed across his face. Little Ah Qing, oh, little Ah Qing. No matter how wily you are, I’m always going to be your Eldest Brother. I can pull a fast one on you without any effort at all. Now, to wrap things up all neat and tidy.

With that thought in mind, Erniu cleared his throat and said, “Let’s not talk about such painful things. Don’t be too sad, little Junior Brother. Just remember that, whatever amazing things you come across in the future, you should always save a portion for me. For example, the flesh of gods, cultivator authority, godly authority, et cetera. And of course, spirit stones and other mundane items count as well. Naturally, the more you set aside for me the better. It’s not that I’m greedy! No! Rather, the more things you give me, the more deeply my memories will be rooted.”

Xu Qing nodded, rummaged around his bag of holding, and took out a spirit stone which he handed to Erniu.

Erniu quickly took it. However, he didn’t sound very pleased when he said, “Just one?”

Xu Qing’s expression became one of bitterness. “Eldest Brother, in the past when you ate spirit stones, you would always eat one stone at a time. You... forgot that habit already?”

Stunned, Erniu looked at Xu Qing. Xu Qing looked back at him very sincerely.

Erniu hesitated, glanced at the spirit stone, and gave another look at Xu Qing. Suddenly feeling very ferocious, he put the spirit stone in his mouth, crunched it to pieces, and swallowed it.

Then, just as he was about to say something, Xu Qing pulled out a sword and performed a quick bit of magic. Rust instantly covered the sword.

“Huh?” Erniu said suspiciously.

“Eldest brother, whenever you eat spirit stones, you always say that they lack flavor. So you follow them up with a rusty sword....”

After a moment of silence, Erniu laughed heartily. “Oh, you! I was just joking around, little Junior Brother! How could I lose my memories! I’m completely fine!”

Eyes glittering, Xu Qing looked at Erniu and softly said, “Eldest Brother, I’m not sure how much of what you said just now was true, and how much was false. But I can tell that you care very much about that certain name.... Therefore, I have something I need to tell you. I’m going to work hard so that, in the future, nothing bad happens to you or anyone else I care about. If I can’t do that... then I’ll suffer with you.”

Xu Qing’s words entered Erniu’s ears and resonated in his heart. Looking at Xu Qing, he suddenly felt the impulse to throw caution to the wind and tell him everything. He opened his mouth to speak.

Xu Qing shook his head. “You have your secrets, Eldest Brother. I have mine. Master has his.... When an appropriate time comes, then you can tell me. Okay?”

Erniu thought about it, then laughed and nodded vigorously. “Sure!”
