Almost there....

Beyond the world of Revered Ancient, out in the starry sky, a host of holy lands had stirred up a starry tempest. A terrifying aura pulsed around them as they sped toward Revered Ancient. Behind all those holy lands was a statue with eight arms. The area around the statue’s head was full of oscillating distortions. It was just barely possible to see a figure seated cross-legged there.

My home. My apprentice. And also... the Primeval Sea.

1. Xu Qing and Erniu gave the eggs to Wu Jianwu in chapter 932. ☜

2. The term god bastard came up previously in chapters 621, 629.1, 630, and 686. ☜

As Timeruins faded away from the Primeval Sea, the surface of the water went calm. But at the same time, an indescribable sensation of danger began to build up, seemingly out of nowhere. It pulsed through the darkness and gloom, causing ripples to distort the air, and creating a pressure that weighed down on the heart and mind. Chanting drifted faintly from within the water, a sound that could drive someone into madness. It was as if death itself was approaching. This was the Primeval Sea, a location in which danger constantly loomed everywhere.

Xu Qing and Erniu both had very serious expressions on their faces. After traversing this sea for more than a month, and experiencing one strange situation after another, they had personally experienced what that danger was like.

One of them controlled a dharmaship as it sped along, the other sent his senses into the surroundings, while simultaneously performing an incantation gesture that made the ship becoming almost invisible within the surrounding darkness.

The dreadnaught had not survived the process of being devoured by Timeruins. Now, they were forced to switch to a dharmaship to travel. Thankfully, Xu Qing’s godsource provided a bolstering effect that pushed the dharmaship to astonishing levels of speed.

After the time it takes an incense stick to burn, something happened. Perhaps it was luck, or perhaps it was because Timeruins’ aura was disappearing, or maybe it was Erniu’s invisibility magic. Regardless, the end effect was that ‘death’ didn’t come around after all.

As the two of them made their way forward at top speed, they gradually left the Primeval Sea. After about two more hours passed, the sense of danger grew so weak it disappeared.

Xu Qing and Erniu breathed long sighs of relief. However, upon exchanging a glance, they could each see that the other was frowning deeply.

“I have no idea where we are...” Xu Qing said grimly. Previously, they had been paying close attention to their position to make sure they didn’t get lost in the outer sea. But after being devoured by Timeruins, their senses were cut off from the outside. And right now, they were unsure of their current location. All they could see around them was endless darkness.

Erniu sighed. “I wonder how Ol’ Pappy Yu is doing. He didn’t get eaten by Timeruins, but I get the feeling he’s still in the outer sea. And I also get the sense he isn’t doing that well. We really miscalculated. If we’d known things would go like this, we could have come up with a good excuse to not come along.”

Xu Qing thought for a moment, then replied, “I have an idea about how to figure out where we are. The downside is that it’ll probably attract unwanted attention.”

Xu Qing looked at Erniu.

Erniu considered what he’d just said. “How much time will it take, little Ah Qing?”

Xu Qing did a quick calculation. “About the time it takes an incense stick to burn.”

“In that case, no problem! Just give me a moment to make some preparations.” But then Erniu looked at the dharmaship and hesitated. “Any chance you have a smaller boat?”

Xu Qing immediately took out a very small dharmaboat and then put away the dharmaship. Erniu gritted his teeth then punched himself hard in the pit of the stomach, which forced sprays of blood out of his lips as he paced back and forth on the dharmaboat.

Xu Qing wasn’t taken aback at all by this behavior. Over their years together, he had come to realize that his Eldest Brother usually had unlimited supplies of blood to work with.

Before long, the dharmaboat was covered inside and out with Erniu’s blood. Erniu looked a bit pale in the face as he sat down and beckoned at Xu Qing.

“I’m using my own blood to unleash the same invisibility effect as the Wordless words. For an incense stick’s worth of time, we should be totally fine!”

Without a moment of hesitation, Xu Qing closed his eyes, sent his god perception out and activated his godly authority of sound. Ripples spread out as... Xu Qing’s god perception detected sound on the quiet outer sea. It was the sound of the water, flowing through the darkness. It was the unknown chanting coming from the ruins that dotted the surface of the sea.

Countless sounds exploded, all at the same time. As time passed, and as the sounds spread, terrifying entities sent out streams of divine will. There was laughter. There was crying. There were polite inquiries. There were enraged shouts.

The many sounds caused Xu Qing to tremble. All he could do was work as hard as possible to screen them out, and send his godly authority further and further out, hoping to identify his position and find the way back. As the process continued, pressure built up, until the dharmaboat started shaking. Erniu felt incomparably nervous, and began spitting out more and more blood to bolster the invisibility effect. Before long, an incense stick’s worth of time had passed.

Xu Qing’s eyes shot open, and he coughed up a mouthful of blood. After, his eyes glittered as he pointed in a specific direction.

“That’s the way to the inner sea!”

Without a moment’s pause, Erniu helped Xu Qing bolster the dharmaboat and send it racing in that direction.

Time slipped by slowly but surely. Half a month.

More time passed. Soon it was a full month since they had been devoured by Timeruins.

They were now about 40,000,000 kilometers to the east of where they had encountered Timeruins. As Xu Qing’s dharmaboat zipped along, the sea water suddenly erupted upward in a huge geyser. The water seemed to fly all the way up into heaven, as if it came from the seafloor itself. In fact, the dharmaboat was carried by the water high into the sky.

Xu Qing and Erniu hadn’t even recovered from their shock when a voice like flowing waves reached their ears.

“Have the two of you been having fun?”

A red mist sprang up, surrounding Xu Qing and Erniu. Then it disappeared into the distance.

Inside the red mist, a figure appeared in front of the dharmaboat, facing away from Xu Qing and Erniu. The figure was tall and straight as a pine tree, with a crimson robe and an extraordinary disposition. This person was Yu Liuchen, who also... had ceased to show any signs of being anxious.

The moment Xu Qing saw Yu Liuchen, he relaxed a bit inwardly. Clasping hands, he bowed.

“Well met, Senior.”

Erniu actually looked excited. “Senior! You finally came!”

Yu Liuchen slowly turned around, revealing a face as handsome as before the moment they had all gone out to sea. Yu Liuchen was also smiling mysteriously, as if everything that had played out had been orchestrated by hīm.

“Did you have fun playing around in my story?”

Xu Qing blinked a few times. He didn’t see how Yu Liuchen’s story could possibly have touched on the mysterious Fifth Star Ring, or the old man from there. As a result, he came to the conclusion that Yu Liuchen was exaggerating a bit. That said, considering that Yu Liuchen had found them, it did seem to imply that they were part of the story. Therefore, he made sure to plaster a dazed and incredulous look onto his face.

It didn’t take any communication for Erniu to pick up on Xu Qing’s train of thought, and thus, he also revealed a dazzled expression, which quickly turned into a display of astonishment and shock.

“Wait a second, sir!” he said loudly. “Senior, are you telling me that everything we went through was actually part of your story? Senior, your words are orders to hordes of gods! Countless grues can be sucked into one of your stories and not even realize what’s happening! Godly might like that... well, Senior, it’s no wonder you’re worshiped by so many other gods. You can make heaven and earth lose their luster. You can make the starry sky glitter brightly for the most consummately powerful god imaginable!” After finishing with his brown-nosing, Erniu immediately asked, “In that case... are we going to continue the fishing expedition?”

When Yu Liuchen heard the words ‘continue the fishing expedition,’ hīs heart flip-flopped. However, hē didn’t reveal that in hīs facial expression, which remained the same as ever. It was almost as if hē had forgotten the instances along the way in which hē had served tea. Looking Xu Qing and Erniu up and down, hē said, “That won’t be necessary. Hē showed up already. Your task is complete.”

With that, Yu Liuchen turned around, faced the vast sea, and stepped up toward the canopy of heaven. High in the sky, hē flicked hīs sleeve, giving the dharmaboat a blessing of godly power that sent it racing away. At the same time, hīs voice echoed out, carrying with it some sort of karma.

“Brilliant Heaven had a god who perished at the hands of the Summer Immortals, whose true body collapsed, whose god perception went dark, and whose true name returned to the starry sky.

“After ten thousand years, that name reappeared. After another ten thousand years, that god perception returned. After another ten thousand years, the true body was restored... call it a cycle. After many cycles, the true name shone brightly in the desire to return from the void.

“The journey was difficult. Unknown beings appeared and were devoured, one after another. More dangers appeared. More were devoured. After many bitter experiences, and many collapses, godsource once again overflowed! The limit was surpassed. Due to incomparable weakness, the True God could not be, and struggled on the verge of Altar God!”

As Yu Liuchen spoke, hīs godly authority spread, fusing with the dome of heaven, imprinting on the sea below, and making true words that described a true name.

“And now, as the fire of rebirth burns above the Primeval Sea, the god longs for rest, to recuperate for hundreds of thousands of years.... But there is tribulation in that god’s life, and that tribulation is in the form of a god. Yu Liuchen!

“Yu Liuchen used the karma of the Summer Immortals to throw out two humans as bait. They experienced two months of time, pulling the True God out of the Primeval Sea... to appear in the open! The god appeared, with weak godly might, god power at the lower limit, a true name blurred, hardly able to remember anything.”

As hīs words echoed out, they caused rumbling sounds to fill heaven and earth. Angry waves surged across the sea, and howls spread everywhere. But Yu Liuchen stood tall in the canopy of heaven, voice crashing like heavenly thunder, growing larger and more influential by the moment.

“And then, as Yu Liuchen looked down, the god collapsed, never to exist again!”

The next instant, wild colors flashed and intense rumbling sounds echoed out as hīs true words showed signs of shattering. Yu Liuchen frowned, then continued speaking, having made a slight correction to his story. “But the god’s prestige still existed, and the god struggled to break free from Yu Liuchen’s gaze. Yet Yu Liuchen had prepared long for this moment, and had a gaze of utmost mightiness. Thus, the returned god was devoured!”

The true words rumbled loudly and the sealing cracked. Clearly, this wasn’t enough. “Although the devouring failed, the returned god’s true name became even more unclear. Hardly any was left. Flight was sought, but Yu Liuchen’s plan had considered all possibilities. He was simply waiting for the right moment to give chase!”

This time, though the sealing rumbled loudly, it didn’t crumble. Seeing that, Yu Liuchen continued speaking. “A pursuit... of 137 days would ensure that the returned god’s true name was absorbed, and replaced forever! And because Yu Liuchen recounted this story, and spoke it to completion, hē should be a True God!”

The true words once again showed signs of crumbling. Yu Liuchen’s eyes glittered, and blood-red light shone off hīm to bolster the true words. “And because Yu Liuchen recounted this story, and spoke it to completion, he should be a peak Altar God, with a chance to rise to True God!”

The moment the words were spoken, heavenly thunder rumbled, and the sea surged. Sealing marks glittered brightly, forming truth and reality.

Off in the distance, Xu Qing and Erniu felt their hearts racing. Behind them, the sea was seething, and the sound of endless chanting rose high. It formed an immense pressure which weighed down on the world. The chanting was like an ancient sound echoing about. A pressure like a reconvergence of time began to gather.

High in the dome of heaven, Yu Liuchen’s eyes glittered as hīs plan of tens of thousands of years began to unfold. The protagonist hē had selected for hīs carefully crafted story... was about to appear!

Xu Qing and Erniu hadn’t hesitated for a moment to send the dharmaboat speeding off into the distance. The blessing of Yu Liuchen’s god power provided a measure of protection, and also boosted the ship’s speed. As a result, they were already a great distance away from that area of the sea. However, the lingering fluctuations of the story spoken by Yu Liuchen still reached them, immediately filling them with an intense sensation of deadly crisis!

Focusing inwardly, Xu Qing sent his cultivation base into full rotation, unleashing all of his godsource to bolster the dharmaboat. Erniu was also fully aware that the more distance they covered, the safer they would be, so he held nothing back to keep the defenses going. After all, they were dealing with a former True God, an entity on the same level as a Summer Immortal!

Thanks to their efforts, it was despite the viscous nature of the outer sea water that the dharmaboat got farther and farther away with every instant that passed.

Far behind them, the sea water beneath Yu Liuchen, which was in reality extremely heavy, suddenly exploded up into the air. As it did, a devilish, illusory, and gruish figure shot out of the sea.

The moment it appeared, Xu Qing and Erniu, despite being off in the distance, shook violently from head to toe. Blood sprayed out of both of their mouths as, all while reeling in astonishment, they tried to flee even faster. At the same time, they used their own ways of looking back to see what was happening.

Far in the distance, they saw that superlatively large figure rising up, so huge it could connect heaven to earth. Its physical appearance was that of a half-rotten corpse, pulsing with a strong aura of death. It was grayish-white, and definitely did not look human! Instead, it looked like some sort of humanoid lizard!

The moment it was out in the open, lightning flashed and thunder boomed. Winds screamed as the gruish figure emanated terrifying fluctuations. The sky rippled, and huge waves rolled out over the surface of the water.

Even more gruish was that the figure’s head wasn’t growing off its body. Instead, the figure held its own head in its right hand! As for its other hand, it held an enormous black candle that burned with a black flame. Despite its extremely bizarre appearance, for some unknown reason, it gave off an extremely holy sensation.

Xu Qing and Erniu weren’t able to continue looking for more than a brief moment before their eyes literally exploded. Both of them had amazing healing powers, yet right now, those powers were working sluggishly. What was more, after losing their eyes, they felt as if all senses of observation had been removed. Turning their heads to face forward, they used instinct alone to flee off into the distance.

However, Yu Liuchen hovered in the air, hīs blood-red robe spreading out in all directions over the great sea, causing both the water and the sky to turn bright red. Hīs eyes shone with shining, golden light, all while hīs godly might pulsed around hīm.

This was something that surpassed the Flawless God level. This was... Altar God!

Altar Gods had solitary godly authority! As Yu Liuchen looked down, godly authority spread out.

The karma in the story caused the Brilliant Heaven True God who had returned to weaken visibly. That weakness stretched down into the substructure of this True God. Hē had faced countless dangers on hīs return trip. Although hē had resolved them one after another, in the end, much of hīs essence had dissipated. After returning, hīs godly might was weak. Hīs god power was low. As a result, hē had planned to hole up and recover. But before that could happen, hē had been dragged out into this situation. Most importantly of all was that hīs will had not fully awoken. After all, hē had been dead!

Yu Liuchen had targeted hīm during hīs awakening process, and as a result, hē had forgotten some fifty to sixty percent of hīs true name.

Thus, Yu Liuchen went all out.

As the golden light shone, the returned god acted just as the story had stated. Rumbling sounds echoed out from hīs body as hē started collapsing. Yet an instant later, though that collapse was continuing, hē let loose a howl that could rip apart heaven, causing wild colors to flash as his rotting godly authority began to shine. Unfortunately, hē was still stuck in the story!

Yu Liuchen had prepared well for this moment, and sent all of the blood-red color in the area rushing toward the god to devour hīm.

Of course, the devouring was foreordained to fail, because the story didn’t describe that happening. After some time passed, a shrill cry echoed out as the red color was shredded to pieces, and the returned god burst out of it and raced toward the depths of the Forbidden Sea.

Hīs will had not yet fully awoken, and hē was only continuing to forget hīs true name. As for this attempt to escape, it was an instinct... that came from the description in the story.

“It’s all in the story. And I decided long ago that you are going to be the main character of my choosing. Your story will be the most beautiful story told during this, the first half of my life.”

Yu Liuchen licked hīs lips, looked at the fleeing god, and then took a step forward. Hē was prepared for this chase to last for 137 days. It couldn’t be one more day than that, nor one less day. It was only on the 137th day that hē could devour the returned god, and then extract the forgotten true name from the corpse.

In doing that... Yu Liuchen could replace this god! And then hīs story would achieve the most beautiful of endings. After all, hē had told this story to completion. Therefore, upon bringing hīs cultivation base back to its peak, hē had advanced another step toward making True God a reality.

“True God....”

Yu Liuchen’s redness swept through the sky over the sea, and off into the distance.

***

Elsewhere on the great sea, Erniu’s eye cavities were slowly filling in with flesh.

“I might have lost my senses, but I still have a premonition that Ol’ Pappy Yu is going to succeed at becoming a True God. The ol’ punk’s godly authority is really far too gruish. That said, Ol’ Pappy Yu is just too stingy! He was using us as bait, and in the end, he hooked the fish! Yet he didn’t give us even a single thing to keep as a souvenir.”

Xu Qing didn’t reply. His eyes had also exploded, but he was recovering faster than Erniu. He could already see a bit of their surroundings, and his other senses were recovering quickly. He pushed the dharmaboat onward with a bit more speed.

“Am I right, little Ah Qing?” Erniu said. He clearly wasn’t very happy.

“Yeah,” Xu Qing replied perfunctorily. “Too stingy.”

Erniu had the habit of not paying much attention to the tone Xu Qing used, and thus he ignored his perfunctory tone. After a moment of thought, he apparently made a decision. “That said, now that I think about it, this experience actually taught us a lot about how to hook fish. In the future, if we ever have a chance, we could find some bait of our own, and go on our own fishing expedition!”

As Xu Qing piloted the dharmaboat onward, he casually asked, “What kind of bait are you talking about? And what kind of fish?”

Erniu flashed a pleased look. “There’s almost too much to choose from when it comes to bait. How about Ningyan? Little Jianjian would work well also. As for what fish to target... well I need to put some thought into that. Have any suggestions, Little Ah Qing?”

Xu Qing shook his head and was about to say something when, all of a sudden, his expression flickered, and he looked at the distant sky ahead of them. His pupils constricted.

Erniu’s eyes hadn’t recovered yet, so he couldn’t see anything. Upon noticing that Xu Qing wasn’t responding to him, he inquisitively asked, “What’s up? Are you really bullying poor old me who has no eyes?”

Voice grim, Xu Qing said, “Eldest Brother... the sky over the inner sea is on fire.”

Reflected within his pupils was the sea of flames visible in the distance.

***

In the Summer Departure calendar of humankind, at the end of the first year of the imperial reign, burning flames fell from the sky and spread to the east, west, south and north of Revered Ancient. The fire came from the starry sky, whipping a starry tempest into a storm of flames. It came as sixteen majestic celestial-level holy lands came to Revered Ancient.

The holy lands were built by the emperors who left years ago with Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity. Every species who left had one of their own.

In the tens of thousands of years that passed since the departure, some of them faded into decay, while some were absorbed by others. As a result, there were fewer now than in the early days. For various reasons, emperors who had established the original holy lands began to perish or go missing. As a result, a classification system for holy lands was established.

Heavenly. Earthly. Celestial. Terrestrial.

The difference between each of the four categories was as great as the difference between heaven and earth. The terrestrial-level holy lands didn’t have any cultivators who were Grand Emperors. But every celestial-level one... did have a Grand Emperor! And those which were in the earthly-level had more than one!

After all, in the ancient past, although Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity had conquered Revered Ancient, that didn’t mean that humans were the only species that occupied the mainland. Species dotted the lands like trees in a forest. Not all species had a Grand Emperor, but those who left with Dark Serenity to establish holy lands beyond the heavens all did.

As of now, species that had left countless years ago were returning. Among them were sixteen celestial-level holy lands that were following the terrestrial-level ones that had already come to Revered Ancient.

In each of the cardinal directions of Revered Ancient, the east, west, south and north, there were four!

Astonishingly, three of them appeared in the sky over the lands of the Firemoon Darkheavens in the east. As for the fourth, it arrived... in the Imperial Region of humankind, right outside the imperial capital!

The arrival of these new holy lands played out completely differently than when the terrestrial-level holy lands had come. These sixteen celestial-level holy lands did one thing upon their arrival: they waged war! And now, the terrestrial-level holy lands didn’t need to put on a front, and they also went on the offensive.

It was in the first year of the reign of Summer Departure that war broke out. It wasn’t an unexpected turn of events to the species of Revered Ancient. Many species were prepared for it, and that was especially true in the east. They had revealed their true intentions thanks to the search for Xu Qing.

In addition, considering that the terrestrial-level holy lands had been driven out of the east, the humans and Firemoons didn’t have to scramble to react. They were ready. The united forces of the east demarcated heaven and earth, thus ensuring that the flames of war didn’t affect the majority of the lands below.

It was around that time that Xu Qing and Erniu approached the inner sea after their ordeal in the Primeval Sea.

***

In Fardark County, outside of the Imperial Region of humankind, a figure shot at top speed toward human territory. He was in extremely bad shape, with his aura unstable. He had numerous internal injuries, and yet, he had seven or eight heads hanging from a rope tied to his waist.

Those two whores Lan Yao and Yue Dong just won’t stop chasing me!

This person looked exhausted and also anxious. Yet despite that, he still looked as deadly as a viper.

And I can’t believe that the Devilbird holy land is one of the ones that arrived here in human territory.

Lan Yao’s clan is extremely powerful in the Devilbird holy land. And her husband is an apprentice of their Grand Emperor! The arrival of this holy land might as well be a death sentence for me.

In that case... I’m going to be worth more than ever to the locals. After all, the Devilbird holy land has a lot of secrets, and I know them all. Since they want to kill me, then my best bet is to seek asylum with the humans, and sell out the damned holy land!

Feng Lintao’s eyes glittered with crafty light as he accelerated.

The holy lands were profoundly meaningful to the species of Revered Ancient. Some people longed for them, while others hated them. In the end, they were the subject of many complicated feelings. Perhaps if time had just continued to pass, the species of Revered Ancient would eventually have stopped thinking so much about the holy lands, and would have ultimately forgotten them. There definitely wasn’t anyone who could have guessed that in the short space of one year... the holy lands would suddenly come back and start waging war.

Thanks to the warfare, suffering spread through Revered Ancient. The confusion, anger, defiance, killing intent, and of course the hatred that had been brewing in Revered Ancient for tens of thousands of years... now began to boil over.

Years ago, the holy lands had left, taking the best and brightest with them. They had taken hope with them. Now they were back, acting high and mighty. And they brought war with them. Thus, the species of Revered Ancient fought back. In the east, west, south and north, the top species issued calls to action, and the response was immediate.

Different actions were taken in different areas. In some places, there was open fighting. Divine abilities were unleashed, and magical techniques raged. In other areas, defenses were erected that contained the scale of the war.

The actions of the east ensured that they controlled the initiative and the rhythm of the war. In fact, at almost the exact same moment as the four celestial-level holy lands descended from heaven wreathed in flames, ninety-nine beams of light shot up from the east. They formed an extremely unique grand spell formation that combined the power of many species, and also tapped into the local mutagen, to cover the east of the mainland, including the continent of South Phoenix and the surrounding inner sea. It prevented the ousted terrestrial-level holy lands from returning, and created a boundary between heaven and earth.

As a result, the four celestial-level holy lands were forced to stop outside the defenses.

At the same time, mutagen became one of the most important tactics used by the east, as it was sent out into the sky to invade the holy lands.

Empress Summer Departure showed up personally, along with the three gods of the Firemoons. By using the Everlasting Dagger-Axe as well as the Dawning Suns humankind had prepared for use in war, thēy were able to engage in battle at a peak level with the holy lands’ Grand Emperors.[1]

The battle lasted for seven days. During that time, the dome of heaven descended into a state like primal-chaos. An abstract painting once again appeared there, filling the sky. Mortals didn’t have any way of understanding what it meant, nor any clue about who had the upper hand or who was losing. But after seven days passed, the three gods returned and went into secluded meditation. Empress Summer Departure appeared to have come out of the fight completely unscathed. It wasn’t possible to determine the state of the four holy lands’ Grand Emperors. And yet, after that battle, the four of them behaved similarly to the three gods. They weren’t seen publicly.

A month passed.

With the initiative they had, the Firemoons and the humans launched small-scale counter offensives. At the same time, the holy lands cultivators occasionally used special magics to break into the spell formation and try to destroy the formation nodes. But the species of the east had special forces units assigned to track such invaders down and kill them. One of the special forces cultivators who earned some merit in various missions was Feng Lintao.

Half a month earlier when he reached human territory, he had revealed his identity and asked for an audience with Empress Summer Departure. The empress hadn’t immediately granted his request. Instead, shē assigned him to one of the special forces units, and gave him a mission to hunt down invaders.

It went without saying that Feng Lintao, in the interests of securing asylum, went above and beyond in fulfilling his duty. His efforts alone resulted in dozens of invaders being killed. He didn’t hold anything back, going so far as to kill members of his own species with incomparable ruthlessness. Whenever he killed an enemy, he would take their head and hang it from his waist. In the end, there were so many heads they were like a long skirt that looked absolutely horrendous and ghastly.

After working hard for about half a month, the empress finally summoned him for a meeting.

At the moment, he stood outside a grand hall in the imperial capital, standing there respectfully, his eyes shining with excitement and fervor, but his heart as cold as ice.

I’ve heard a lot about this human empress. Shē converted from being a cultivator to being a god. And not just some low-level god. Shē used the power of the successive human emperors to become an Altar God....

This empress is no simpleton.... That said, the less simple a person is, the more confident they’ll be. And from a certain perspective, someone like that... will be perfect for the plan I’ve prepared to get out of this mess.

Feng Lintao glanced down at the skirt of severed heads. They were a blood tribute that he had prepared specially for this moment. He had put a lot of thought into his decision to defect to the humans. All of his analyses had led him to the conclusion there was only one way for him to get out of his current mess.

I need to make myself valuable. I need to prove my loyalty.

Feng Lintao narrowed his eyes. He was well aware that a god could easily read his thoughts. That... was why he was thinking such things. In fact, even as he mentally pondered such things, a tranquil voice echoed out from within the grand hall.

“Feng Lintao is hereby summoned for an imperial audience.”

Feng Lintao’s expression turned very serious. After clasping hands and bowing in the direction of the hall, he walked into the grand hall. Once inside, he saw over a hundred human cultivators standing in four rows, looking at him. Directly in front of him was a large staircase, with chairs on each level. The chairs closest to the bottom were for heavenly marquises, while those higher up were for heavenly kings.

At the very top, the empress sat expressionlessly on a majestic imperial throne.

Standing to the side of the empress was a person clad in the robe of the crown prince. He was none other than Ningyan. After becoming the crown prince, he always stood in that position, not to learn management skills, but rather, to observe. That was what his mother had asked of him. Right now, he was observing this holy lands cultivator who had defected to humankind.

“Feng Lintao, offer greetings to the human empress, Summer Departure!”

Feng Lintao retracted his gaze and bowed at the waist to the empress. When he straightened, he waved his right hand to toss the severed heads down in front of him.

“Your Majesty,” he said, “this is a blood tribute for you. Among them are scions of some of the great clans from the holy lands. All of them are highly ranked. Of course, I’m well aware that this won’t be enough to prove my loyalty. Therefore, I’ve come prepared to reveal two bits of classified information to you!

“The first bit of information is this: A thousand years ago, the Devilbird holy land was not celestial-class. It was the weakest of the earthly-level holy lands. That was because it didn’t always have one Grand Emperor. Back then, it had two!

“A thousand years ago, Patriarch Devilbird, who was at the peak of Grand Emperor, tried to break out of the Quasi-Immortal level and become a Summer Immortal. The breakthrough failed. The patriarch’s body wasted away, and his soul scattered. After preparing a legacy to leave behind, he entered meditation to die.

“When he perished, the Devilbird holy land was reduced to the celestial level. That said, there are rumors that Patriarch Devilbird might actually be able to recover. Your Majesty, I hope you will take precautions in this regard.”

There were many in the crowd who reacted to Feng Lintao’s words with visible surprise. After he finished with his first bit of classified information, he paused briefly. Then he continued, “The second bit of information relates to the holy lands’ reason for returning....”

The moment the words left his mouth, all eyes became focused solely on him. Seeing that, Feng Lintao settled his energy and cleared his mind.

“They have three reasons.

“First. They’re planning to abandon Revered Ancient forever, and never return. Before doing so, they want to take all the resources away!

“Second. They want to carry out a blood sacrifice, and for that, they need a huge stockpile of resources. That’s why they’ve immediately started waging war.

“Third. They were ordered to come here! And the person who issued the orders was not Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity. The truth is that the Ancient Emperor went missing about two thousand years ago. After that, the holy lands had no leader, and devolved into chaos. What’s more, two thousand years ago, one of the ancient Summer Immortals who left Revered Ancient... came back!”

The echoing words provoked an immediate stir among the cultivators in the grand hall.

This news was monumental. That was especially true considering it touched one of the ancient Summer Immortals. Because of that, the initial reaction was one of shock and disbelief.

“Because of my low status, I have no way of knowing this Summer Immortal’s name. The name is taboo, after all. But thanks to the back-channel information I have access to... I heard that this returned individual has a cultivation base at the very peak of the Summer Immortal level. In fact, it might have already surpassed that level, meaning that it exists in a level that can only be described as freakish and unimaginable.

“Some have said that this level is equivalent to that of the Brilliant Heaven god emperor. That’s the level above True God, which is God Lord. In the cultivator system, that level designation is called Immortal Lord.

“Apparently, though, his cultivation base is unstable, which is the reason for his return to the holy lands. He has demanded that the holy lands scour Revered Ancient for something that can stabilize his cultivation base. As for the blood sacrifice, it will be used to summon that item, whatever it is. The more blood used in the sacrifice, the more accurate the summons can be. Unfortunately, I’m not completely sure of what that item is.

“However, there’s one thing I can be certain of. This half-step Immortal Lord found an item that can temporarily bypass the blockade created by the broken face. In other words, it’s a way to leave Revered Ancient. That’s one of the main reasons that the holy lands have dared to come here.”

Feng Lintao’s explanation provoked more than a few gasps from the humans in the grand hall. It wasn’t that their willpower was lacking. Rather, this information was just too monumentally shocking. Even Ningyan was breathing heavily, and couldn’t help but glance a few times at his mother.

Feng Lintao took that all in and felt very pleased. He wasn’t lying in anything he’d said. Every word was true. And he was convinced that his information would prove that he was sincere in defecting to humankind.

However, he also knew that he needed to prove that the choices he had made were logical. In other words, he needed to explain why he had chosen to defect. With that thought in mind, he clasped hands and bowed again in the direction of the empress, who had still not reacted in any way.

“Your Majesty, the reason I’m being so candid, and the reason I’m explaining all of these things, is that the Devilbird holy land has treated me with great insensitivity. I have two archenemies there. One is named Yue Dong, and she’s a vicious and treacherous woman who will stop at nothing to see me dead.

“The other is named Lan Yao, and she has the heart like that of a snake or scorpion. She comes from one of the five great clans of the Devilbird holy land, and her husband is an apprentice of the very same Patriarch Devilbird who went into secluded meditation to die. In the Devilbird holy land, I’m considered to have impure blood, which is why I was always looked down on. Later, I offended them, which is the same as offending half of the entire holy land. Ever since then, they’ve been chasing me nonstop in the hopes of killing me.

“That’s why I defected to humankind! Your Majesty, I don’t expect you to take all of this at face value. My conflict with Lan Yao and Yue Dong was witnessed by two human cultivators. Based on what I could tell, both of them are important people who are most likely famous among you humans!”

Feng Lintao finished speaking and kept his eyes on the empress. Everyone in the grand hall similarly looked at the empress with very serious expressions on their faces.

Looking back at Feng Lintao, the empress calmly said, “What are the names of the two human cultivators who saw all of this?”

Feng Lintao immediately responded, “One of them called himself Sir Firedark, and he was traveling with his Elder Brother. Upon reflection, I’m fairly certain he was using a fake name. As for their true identities... thankfully, I managed to get a bit of information recently.”

With that, he waved his hand, causing two projected images to form. One of them wore a blue robe and stood tall, with eyes glittering like heavenly bodies, and extremely attractive facial features. The other wore a similar blue robe, but had plain facial features and a rather shifty expression.

Feng Lintao clearly didn’t like the second person. He was the one who had pretended to be hovering on the brink of death, all for the purpose of stealing Feng Lintao’s sageheaven god vine.

As soon as the two images appeared, strange expressions appeared on the faces of everyone in the grand hall. In particular, Ningyan’s eyes went wide.

Taking a deep breath, Feng Lintao calmly said, “Therefore, Your Majesty, all you have to do is ask these two, and they’ll confirm the truth of everything I told you.”

***

Out on the Primeval Sea, Erniu sneezed.

“Some lowlife must be talking about me!” he said. Erniu’s eyes had grown back, and he now reclined comfortably on the dharmaboat.

Xu Qing ignored him as he sat cross-legged and meditated, all while assessing the ways he had transformed recently. His godsource was stronger than before he had come out to sea. His godly authority was also a bit more majestic than before. All of it was thanks to those meat skewers he had eaten. The flesh of Timeruins was understandably extraordinary.

The most astonishing improvement was to his soul. His soul was now much tougher than before, by many times over. And the benefit from the nourishment was continuing. His god perception had improved dramatically, and his godly senses were stronger. In addition, the connection between his soul and his fleshly body had improved.

My battle prowess has benefited similarly.

A short time later, he ended the day’s session of meditation, opened his eyes, and looked in the direction of the inner sea.

“We’ll arrive soon,” he murmured.

The two of them had traveled at top speed for a month, pushing the dharmaboat to get back home. Although they had encountered a few dangerous situations, none had posed any challenge. Whether that was because of luck or because of the blessing Yu Liuchen had given them when they parted, it was hard to tell. As of now, they were only about half a day away from the inner sea.

Upon realizing how close they were to the inner sea, Erniu started getting himself back in shape. After all, he was the type of person who liked to look good. Although he couldn’t get rid of his fur, he didn’t think like normal people. In fact, that was one of his talents. As such, he took all of that dark fur and braided it together to form something like a coat of fur armor....

Xu Qing couldn’t help but admire Erniu when he saw that.

Several hours later, they reached the boundary between the outer sea and the inner sea. As black mist roiled, the ship shot across the border. Once they were in the inner sea, a burst of spell formation power swept over them. Almost as quickly, it vanished, allowing them to enter the inner sea smoothly.

The sunlight was dazzling. The sea breeze was warm.

Clouds roiled above as a figure like an eagle or a phoenix appeared, whistling down toward them. Along the way, it turned into Huang Yan, who landed on the surface of the water and glared angrily at Xu Qing.

“So, you’ve finally returned, huh? I promised Elder Sister to take you back safely, only for you to go missing again. Do you know how much face I lost, Xu Qing?”

Hearing that caused Xu Qing to break into a smile.

Huang Yan hurried forward and boarded the dharmaboat. Upon seeing Erniu, a quizzical expression appeared on his face.

“You went out to sea and came back with a fur coat? What is it you call an ox with a bunch of fur? A yak, right?”[2]

Erniu smiled sarcastically. “What the hell do you know, you old bird? Have you ever been to the outer sea? I don’t think so. Let me tell you, this is the most popular fashion among the species there!”

Glaring, Huang Yan waved his hand, causing a tornado to pop into being right on top of Erniu, which then sent him flying several thousand kilometers off into the distance.

Huang Yan grinned. “Finally, we can have some peace and quiet. Alright, Xu Qing, let’s go home! By the way, Elder Sister wanted me to tell you... that quite a few people are awaiting your return.” Huang Yan then cleared his throat. “And they’re women....”

1. The Everlasting Dagger-Axe was previously mentioned in chapters 902 and 953. ☜

2. Although I think this yak joke is funny in English, it’s slightly funnier in Chinese. As most of you should remember, the niu in Erniu’s name means ox. And in Chinese, the word for yak combines the character for fur with the character for ox. So a yak is a furry ox or a furred ox. ☜

The canopy of heaven was auspicious and peaceful. The light of the setting sun shone over the inner sea, making it seem like there was a gorgeous painting filling the sky over South Phoenix and the Forbidden Sea. Profound colors and mysterious charm brought out the splendor and complexity of life. Gradually, it became part of the afterglow of sunset that spread out over the sea, filling its darkness with scintillating waves.

As twilight settled over the lands, it reached the Seven Blood Eyes port, where waves gently lapped against the reefs and rocks, creating a muffled thrum that indicated night had come. The sea breeze blew softly through the evening, caressing the various ships in the harbors, and brushing against the faces of cultivators from various sects and species.

Eventually, it reached Ding Xue, causing her long, beautiful hair to sway out in front of her. It caused the little bells on the box next to Yanyan to tinkle. And in a medicine shop overlooking the sea was a graceful figure whose long skirt stirred in the gentle wind.[1]

Ding Xue stood next to the water at the port, clad in a form-fitting gown that accentuated her beautiful curves, but at the same time, did nothing to diminish the heroic air she had manifested years ago. It was as if the passage of time hadn’t changed her at all. She had a bronze sword strapped to her back.

A short distance behind Ding Xue was Zhao Zhongheng, who was still as infatuated with her as he’d always been.[2]

Yanyan currently sat on the wooden box on a dharmaboat in the very same harbor that Xu Qing had used when he first arrived in Seven Blood Eyes. Harbor 79. Next to her were five large water barrels which emanated the scent of blood. Her eyes were narrowed and her lips pursed. Her gaze was one of keen anticipation.[3]

There were others waiting besides these women. They included numerous Seven Blood Eyes disciples, including Violent Crimes Division constables from various mountain peaks.

Time slipped by slowly but surely. Night fell. Lanterns lit the port like little stars, making the place look almost like a shining starry sky. The ‘starlight’ glittered on the surface of the water, creating a resplendent painting. Within that painting, a solitary dharmaboat shot across the water.

Xu Qing stood at the prow looking at the familiar Seven Blood Eyes, as well as all the familiar faces there. He spotted Ding Xue, and he spotted Yanyan.

The disciples gathered at the port started calling out “Fourth Highness!”

At the same time, Second Elder Sister emerged from the Seventh Peak and went down to the port. She arrived just as the dharmaboat was pulling in.

Huang Yan jumped out and rushed over to her, looking very pleased with himself, as if he were saying, “See! I told you I’d bring your little Junior Brother back!”

Elder Sister chuckled and looked at Xu Qing. “Welcome home, little Junior Brother.”

***

Familiar auras. Familiar surroundings. Familiar mountain peaks.

After reconnecting with old friends and acquaintances, Xu Qing left Huang Yan and Second Elder Sister to have their own reunion, and strode through the night to his mansion grotto. Although he hadn’t stayed long in this mansion grotto, as soon as he sat down, he felt tranquil and calm. His heart, which had been racing for so long now, finally became peaceful.

He thought back to everything that happened over the better part of the last year. First he ran into Floating Fiend, then destroyed the Vivifiend holy land. After, he chased down Floating Fiend... then went with Yu Liuchen to the outer sea, where he had faced one dangerous situation after another. The entire time he had felt taut with anxiety and fear.

Now that he was back in Seven Blood Eyes, he could let loose a long sigh. That said, he knew that this period of rest wouldn’t last for very long. His stay in Seven Blood Eyes would be a short one.

War had already broken out, and as the region lord of both the Holytide Region and the Nightspirit Region, he was like the heart and soul of Sea-Sealing County. Now that he was back, he needed to go present himself to the empress and join the war effort that affected the entire east of Revered Ancient. He also needed a tempering of blood and death to continue to fuse his fleshly body and soul. At the same time, he required deeper enlightenment of his godly authority.

My dreadnaught was so badly damaged I can’t use it anymore. I guess I need to see if Zhang San can fix it.

After mulling everything over, he closed his eyes and focused on cultivation. The profound sun immortal light flowed within him, like a sun rising inside his body. It cast dazzling light and warmth into him, which then returned to the sun, creating a cycle. The process brought his godsource into play, and illuminated the one thousand godly authority lineaments.

Time passed slowly but surely.

Two hours later, he opened his eyes and looked at the door of the mansion grotto, his brow slightly furrowed.

A voice echoed from outside. “Is now a good time, Elder Brother Xu Qing? I cooked some sweet potato and peanut congee for you.”

The voice was deliberately soft, and seemed a bit timid.

Xu Qing was familiar with this voice, and was also familiar with this behavior. This person was obviously Ding Xue. There weren’t many options at hand for Xu Qing. He was not the ignorant kid he had been years ago. He knew full well what Ding Xue was thinking when she looked at him. But when all was said and done, they were fellow disciples of the same sect, so he waved his hand, causing the mansion grotto’s door to swing open silently.

As moonlight spilled inside, a graceful figure strolled through the door.

“It’s been a long time, Big Bro Xu Qing.” Ding Xue’s face was flushed, and every time she blinked, her long eyelashes seemed to recount a moving tale that would stir the heart.

Nearing, she bent down and put the sweet potato and peanut congee down in front of Xu Qing. When she bent, her tight clothing made her attractive figure even more prominent. Her eyes looked like stars shining in the deep night, flickering with mysterious charm.

The passage of time didn’t seem visible on her at all. In fact, it was quite the opposite. She seemed even more beautiful than before. Her eyebrows were more elegant, like graceful willow leaves, imparting a sense of sweet-tempered firmness. Her long, straight nose and delicate, ruby lips would cause just about any man to be hard-pressed to not want to get close to her.

Xu Qing said nothing at first. He saw the anticipation in her eyes, and thought back to how she had treated him years ago.... Sighing softly, he picked up the congee and took a sip.

“Pretty good,” he said. Then he asked her a few questions about her cultivation.

Ding Xue looked at him with her heart pounding. Her plan for this night was to take Xu Qing for her own. That was why she had dressed in this way. But now that she was in front of him, she suddenly felt nervous, and wasn’t sure what to do next. All she could do was answer his questions about cultivation.

Time passed. About an hour later, she left his mansion grotto feeling somewhat confused. Once outside, she realized that her plan to win Xu Qing had failed.

I just need to prepare more thoroughly. Next time... next time I’m definitely going to win Elder Brother Xu Qing for my own! However, I need to keep myself under control. I love him, but that’s my personal matter. I definitely can’t put any pressure on him.

Thumping her chest encouragingly, she took a deep breath and proceeded to encourage herself further as she walked off. She had long since become used to the fact that there was someone following her. In fact, she was as used to him as she was used to the air.

That person was none other than Zhao Zhongheng. He followed her through the night, looking emotional as he thought, Xue’er, I’ve been in love with you for years now. But I know that loving you is my personal matter. Don’t feel any pressure. I don’t want my love for you to be a burden. I just hope that you can always be happy.

Feeling moved by his own words, Zhao Zhongheng took a deep breath and followed her with increased determination.

As was expected, Xu Qing could see all of that playing out. When he thought about how Zhao Zhongheng hadn’t given up even after all these years, he couldn’t help but feel pity. Shaking his head, he closed his eyes and went back to meditating.

And yet, only a moment later, he opened his eyes again and looked to the entrance of the mansion grotto.

A moment later, a trembling voice reached his ears. “Big Bro Xu Qing, my grandma told me what you went through to save me.... I couldn’t track down any holy lands cultivators, but I did catch a few Night Dove agents so you could vent some anger.”

Outside of the mansion grotto was Yanyan, clad in a red robe. She was biting her lip, but no blood seeped out, as she swallowed it all.

***

An hour later, Yanyan left.

Xu Qing sat inside the mansion grotto looking thoughtful. He had become aware earlier that Yanyan had a unique constitution. That, coupled with the fact that she had attracted the gaze of Golden Crow’s musician, sparked certain speculations within Xu Qing.

That night as Yanyan dealt with the Night Dove agents, Xu Qing used his god perception to confirm some of his suspicions.

It’s not that she doesn’t have any mutagen in her. It’s just that the mutagen doesn’t manifest in her fleshly body. Instead, it enters her soul.... As a result, her soul has transformed in a very unique way, allowing it to absorb mutagen. The downside is that she doesn’t understand what to do with it. That’s why following the path of cultivators isn’t working for her. It really disturbs her on an emotional level. In some respects, Yanyan is a natural-born god cultivator! freewebnovel.com

Before Yanyan left, he put some of his own godsource into her soul, creating a seed that would help her in her future cultivation. After more thought on the matter, he closed his eyes and went back to cultivation.

He got no further visitors that night. Eventually, the sun rose.

***

As the sun rose, a figure crawled up onto the shore in the Seven Blood Eyes port, covered with soaking fur. Once out of the water, the furry figure started cursing.

“Huang Yan, you damned old bird! I can’t believe you slapped me that far! And you even sealed my bag of holding and cultivation base so I couldn’t fly. I had to swim the whole way back! You just wait until I track you down!”

This person was, of course, Erniu. Even as he gnashed his teeth, the sky grew bright.

***

As the morning breeze blew across the port, a slight rain fell.

Xu Qing opened an oilskin umbrella as he walked down the Seventh Peak, disguised to look like the low-level disciple he had been years ago. After finding the breakfast stall he had frequented in the past, he bought a bowl of jellied tofu for breakfast. After, he went to Harbor 176 to find Zhang San.

Despite the rain, the city was as busy as ever, with people of all species hastening to and fro. At one point, he walked past a medicine shop he had frequented long ago. Upon passing, he caught sight of a person inside wearing a pale orange robe. She was currently looking down at the pill furnace in front of her as she concocted some medicinal pills.

She was Gu Muqing, who had once been a chosen from the Second Peak, the peak that specialized in alchemy. Back in the day, she got to know Xu Qing after buying some of his white boluses.[4]

Seeing how focused she was, Xu Qing decided not to bother her, and continued on his way.

Inside the shop, Gu Muqing suddenly sensed something and looked up. But the streets were crowded, and with the rain, it was hard to see anything.

They had no reunion. It was not something fated to happen, just like something far in the distance that could never be seized.
